torch.Tensor\n172: ) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:\n173:     \"\"\"\n174:     Casts a tensor from e2m1fn to e4m3fn losslessly.\n175:     \"\"\"\n176:     assert x.dtype == torch.int8\n177:     assert x.ndim == 2\n178:     out_dim, in_dim = x.size()\n179:     in_dim *= 2\n180:     fp8_block_size = 128\n181:     fp4_block_size = 32\n182:     assert in_dim % fp8_block_size == 0 and out_dim % fit in e4m3fn (max 448)\n192:     # 6.0 * 2^6 = 384 < 448; 6.0 * 2^7 = 768 > 448; so MAX_OFFSET_BITS = 6\n193:     MAX_OFFSET_BITS = 6\n194: \n195:     bOut = out_dim // fp8_block_size\n196:     bIn =   # bOut, bIn, 128*4\n204:     offset = scale / scale_max_offset_bits\n205:     # bOut, bIn, 128, 128\n206:     offset = offset.unflatten(-1, (fp8_block_size, -1)).repeat_interleave(\n207:         fp4_block_size, dim=-1\n208:     )\n209:     x = (x * offset).transpose(1, 2).reshape(out_dim, in_dim)\n210:     return x.to(torch.float8_e4m3fn), scale_max_offset_bits.squeeze(-1).to(\n211: tensor from e2m1fn to e4m3fn losslessly.\n    \"\"\"\n    assert x.dtype == torch.int8\n    assert x.ndim == 2\n    out_dim, in_dim = x.size()\n    in_dim *= 2\n    fp8_block_size = 128\n dim=-1).flatten(2)\n\n    # max_fp4 (6.0) * MAX_OFFSET must fit in e4m3fn (max 448)\n    # 6.0 * 2^6 = 384 < 448; 6.0 * 2^7 = 768 > 448; so MAX_OFFSET_BITS = 6\n    MAX_OFFSET_BITS = 6\n\n    bOut = out_dim // fp8_block_size\n    bIn = in_dim // fp8_block_size\n    # bOut, bIn, 128, 128\n    x = x.view(bOut, fp8_block_size, bIn, fp8_block_size).transpose(1, 2)\n    # bOut, bIn, 128*4\n    scale = scale.float().view(bOut, fp8_block_size, bIn, -1).transpose(1, 2).flatten(2)\n    ## bOut, bIn, 1\n    scale_max_offset_bits = scale.amax(dim=-1, keepdim=True) / (2**MAX_OFFSET_BITS)\n    # bOut, bIn,        )\n\n\nclass Fp8LinearMethod(LinearMethodBase):\n    \"\"\"Linear method for FP8.\n\n    It supports the following quantization schemes:\n    - Per-channel weight quantization + per-token \"DEFAULT_QUANTIZATION_FORMAT\",\n]\n\n\nclass QuantizationStatus(str, Enum):\n    \"\"\"\n    Enum storing the different states a quantized layer can be in\n\n    - Initialized: Quantization parameters are initialized to empty values\n    - Calibration: Quantization parameters are being calibrated, observers are attached\n    - Frozen: Quantization parameters are fully calibrated, observers are removed\n    - Compressed: All parameters are quantized to target dtype\n    - Decompressed: Parameters are converted back into frozen state,\n        additionally, weight qdq is skipped during forward passes for better performance\n    \"\"\"\n\n    INITIALIZED = \"initialized\"\n    CALIBRATION = \"calibration\"\n    FROZEN = \"frozen\"\n    COMPRESSED = \"compressed\"\n   \"\"\"\n        return\n\n    def __ge__(self, other):\n        if other is None:\n            return True\n        if not isinstance(other, self.__class__):\n            raise NotImplementedError\n QuantizationConfig(BaseModel):\n    \"\"\"\n    Full configuration specifying how a model is quantized. Each quantized layer is\n    mapped to a QuantizationScheme in config_groups.\n\n    :param config_groups: dict of QuantizationSchemes specifying the quantization\n    settings for each quantized layer. A group could also be a reference to\n    a predefined scheme name, mapped to a list of its target layers/classes\n    :param quant_method: a constant used to differentiate compressed-tensors\n    quantization from other quantization configs\n    :param format: specifies how the quantized model is stored on disk\n    :quantization_status: specifies the current status of all quantized layers. If None, kv cache is not quantized.\n        When applying kv cache quantization to transformer AutoModelForCausalLM,\n        the kv_cache_scheme gets converted into a QuantizationScheme that:\n            - targets the `q_proj` and `k_proj` modules of the model. The outputs\n              of those modules are the keys and values that might be cached\n            - quantizes the outputs of the aformentioned layers, so that\n              keys and values are compressed before storing them in the cache\n        There is an explicit assumption that the model contains modules with\n        `k_proj` and `v_proj` in their names.
